- Given this pattern, the next play in the cycle should be 'scissors'.

- Playing 'paper' against 'scissors' and 'rock' against 'paper' yielded negative rewards.

Based on the cyclic pattern observed, the opponent's strategy seems to be predictable, and I can exploit this by choosing the counter strategy.

**Conclusion:**

- The opponent has played 'rock' twice and 'paper' twice, but 'scissors' only once.

   - Playing scissors has often resulted in negative rewards due to the opponent's preference for rock.
   - Playing rock has been less successful due to the opponent's occasional paper plays.
